```
### Key Requirements and Skills Needed:

1. **Minimum of 7 years of Financial Crime Compliance experience** in a financial institution.

- **Senior**: The role involves leading thematic reviews, providing financial crime advisory advice, and managing deliverables independently. It also requires high-level stakeholder engagement and reporting to senior management.

- **Hybrid**: The job posting mentions flexible working options, including part-time and hybrid working arrangements.

### Growth Potential Assessment:

- **High**: The role involves significant responsibility and leadership, with opportunities for further development in client engagement, risk oversight, and compliance. The company culture also supports personal and professional growth.
```

```
JOB TITLE: Institutional Cash and Trade Engagement, Controls and Risk Oversight team ‚Äì Client Engagement and Solutions - Regional Lead Europe (f/m/x)

JOB POSTING:
Institutional Cash and Trade Engagement, Controls and Risk Oversight team ‚Äì Client Engagement and Solutions - Regional Lead Europe (f/m/x) Job ID:R0388317 Full/Part-Time: Full-time Regular/Temporary: Regular Listed: 2025-06-23 Location: Frankfurt Position Overview Details of the role and how it fits into the teamThe Client Engagement and Solutions (CES) team is responsible for the management of non-financial risks associated with correspondent banking relationships. It assesses potential financial crime and reputational risks of these clients by conducting a holistic analysis of the risks they pose to Deutsche Bank. The team provides advice for business areas in relation to our clients' financial crime compliance programme and considers country-specific, reputational, and geopolitical / PEP risks of maintaining correspondent banking relationships with banks located across the world.Your key responsibilitiesLead thematic (sector or country-specific) or trigger CES-led correspondent banking reviews to gain an understanding of the client sector and jurisdiction risk by:Conducting preliminary analysis of the client and sector and recommending clients for further reviewConducting holistic analysis of banks; assessment of their Anti-Financial Crime (AFC) control and governance structureConducting AFC risk-based transaction analysis reviewsBeing the author and owner of the formal assessment reportProvide financial crime advisory advice based on results of client reviewsPresenting report and formal findings to the appropriate governance councils.Collaborate with Regional CES Team Leads, as well as the local, regional, and global business and AFC network with respect to your own responsibilities, and leading onsite visits with the business at our clients' offices or via conference callsProvision of timely updates and escalation of issues where required to Global Head of CESProvide regular reports to the senior management on the status of non-financial risks, control effectiveness, and compliance mattersYour skills and experiencesMinimum of 7 years of Financial Crime Compliance experience gained from working in a financial institution, with exposure to correspondent banking and good understanding of local and / or international regulatory requirements related to AFC and compliance.Strong knowledge of the AFC control and governance framework implemented within banks including understanding of typical AML and Know Your Client and Sanctions policy/programme requirements (e.g. experience with Transactional Monitoring and Sanctions screening systems).Strong knowledge of SWIFT network and the financial crime risks of processing correspondent bank paymentsExperience working within a global team in a multinational organisation with proven experience in senior stakeholder management engagementHigh level of initiative, strong work ethic and analytical skills, with excellent attention to detail, plus able to work independently to manage deliverables to timely completion.Due to client segment and nature of the role, proficiency in both spoken and written English is required. 1. Required Skills/Qualifications:
```
```
   - Minimum of 7 years Financial Crime Compliance experience in financial institutions, with knowledge in correspondent banking risks and regulatory compliance requirements (e.g., AML policies).
   - Strong understanding of SWIFT network usage and the associated financial crime risks within banks for transaction processing payments to clients overseas. 
   - Demonstrated experience with Transactional Monitoring, Sanctions screening systems along with good governance structures in place at their previous workplace or institutions they've worked for.
   - Proficient communication skills in both spoken and written English due to the multinational nature of correspondent bank relationships across different jurisdictions. 
   
2. Company Culture Indicators:
   - Commitment to shared values, including responsibility, economic thinking, initiative-taking, targeted collaboration as mentioned by Maass in his statement about company culture at Deutsche Bank Group.
   - Celebrating collective successes and maintaining a positive work environment that is inclusive of all individuals regardless of gender or background (indicated through the welcoming nature towards "all men" with an emphasis on fairness). 
   - Emphasis on personal well-being, including mental health awareness trainings to help balance professional and private challenges.
   
3. Role Complexity Level: Senior (due to leadership responsibilities in thematic or trigger CES reviews)

4. Remote Work Compatibility: Yes/Hybrid (implied by the company's offer of flexible working options, though not explicitly stated for this position).

5. Growth Potential Assessment: The role entails leading a team and conducting in-depth reviews which could be seen as demonstrating high responsibility within senior compliance roles at Deutsche Bank Group with potential career development opportunities given the leadership responsibilities mentioned alongside job requirements (although specific growth path is not detailed).
```

```
   - Minimum of 7 years Financial Crime Compliance experience in a financial institution with correspondent banking exposure, including understanding local/international AFC regulatory requirements (e.g., Transactional Monitoring).
   - Strong knowledge of the Anti-Financially Crime control and governance framework within banks; familiarity with typical Money Laundering and Sanctions policies such as Know Your Client standards, including SWIFT network experience for processing correspondent bank payments.
   - Proven senior stakeholder management engagement skills in a multinational setting.
   - Strong work ethic, attention to detail, analytical thinking abilities with the ability to independently manage deliverables and timely reporting on non-financial risks control effectiveness and compliance matters.
   - Proficiency in both spoken and written English is mandatory due to international client segments.

2. Company Culture Indicators:
   - Commitment to a mindset of shared responsibility, economic thinking, initiative taking, focused collaboration for Deutsche Bank‚Äôs success as part of the Group family.
   - Celebrating individual and team achievements together within an inclusive environment promoting diversity, equity, and inclusion (DEI).
   - Focus on mental health with support provided in difficult life situations through consultations or trainings aimed at maintaining balance between work-life demands.
   - Emphasis on physical wellbeing by offering access to regular checkups and promoting a balanced diet, alongside facilities like fitness centers for staff use as part of personal health maintenance initiatives.
   
3. Role Complexity Level: Senior (the job requires substantial experience in financial crime compliance with managerial duties.)

4. Remote Work Compatibility: No direct mention; however, the company culture emphasizes physical and mental wellbeing which could imply a need for on-site visits‚Äîpotentially indicating limited remote work options or at least regular site presence is important during reviews and client interactions as suggested by leading onsite visits.
   
5. Growth Potential Assessment: With leadership responsibilities, including heading thematic/country-specific CES teams for correspondent banking review assessments that have global impacts due to their risk nature across different jurisdictions and countries in Europe‚Äîthis indicates significant growth potential within a regional or even potentially international scope.
```

```
JOB TITLE: Institutional Cash and Trade Engagement, Controls and Risk Oversight team ‚Äì Client Engagement and Solutions - Regional Lead Europe (f/m/x)

JOB POSTING:
Institutional Cash and Trade Engagement, Controls and Risk Oversight team ‚Äì Client Engagement and Solutions - Regional Lead Europe (f/m/x) Job ID:R0388317 Full/Part-Time: Full-time Regular/Temporary: Regular Listed: 2025-06-23 Location: Frankfurt Position Overview Details of the role and how it fits into the teamThe Client Engagement and Solutions (CES) team is responsible for the management of non-financial risks associated with correspondent banking relationships. It assesses potential financial crime and reputational risks of these clients by conducting a holistic analysis of the risks they pose to Deutsche Bank. The team provides advice for business areas in relation to our clients' financial crime compliance programme and considers country-specific, reputational, and geopolitical / PEP risks of maintaining correspondent banking relationships with banks located across the world.Your key responsibilitiesLead thematic (sector or country-specific) or trigger CES-led correspondent banking reviews to gain an understanding of the client sector and jurisdiction risk by:Conducting preliminary analysis of the client and sector and recommending clients for further reviewConducting holistic analysis of banks; assessment of their Anti-Financial Crime (AFC) control and governance structureConducting AFC risk-based transaction analysis reviewsBeing the author and owner of the formal assessment reportProvide financial crime advisory advice based on results of client reviewsPresenting report and formal findings to the appropriate governance councils.Collaborate with Regional CES Team Leads, as well as the local, regional, and global business and AFC network with respect to your own responsibilities, and leading onsite visits with the business at our clients' offices or via conference callsProvision of timely updates and escalation of issues where required to Global Head of CESProvide regular reports to the senior management on the status of non-financial risks, control effectiveness, and compliance mattersYour skills and experiencesMinimum of 7 years of Financial Crime Compliance experience gained from working in a financial institution, with exposure to correspondent banking and good understanding of local and / or international regulatory requirements related to AFC and compliance.Strong knowledge of the AFC control and governance framework implemented within banks including understanding of typical AML and Know Your Client and Sanctions policy/programme requirements (e.g. experience with Transactional Monitoring and Sanctions screening systems).Strong knowledge of SWIFT network and the financial crime risks of processing correspondent bank paymentsExperience working within a global team in a multinational organisation with proven experience in senior stakeholder management engagementHigh level of initiative, strong work ethic and analytical skills, with excellent attention to detail, plus able to work independently to manage deliverables to timely completion.Due to client segment and nature of the role, proficiency in both spoken and written English is required. JOB POSTING:
```
```
Institutional Cash and Trade Engagement, Controls and Risk Oversight team ‚Äì Client Engagement and Solutions - Regional Lead Europe (f/m/x) Job ID:R0388317 Full/Part-Time: Full-time Regular/Temporary: Regular Listed: 2025-06-23 Location: Frankfurt Position Overview Details of the role and how it fits into the teamThe Client Engagement and Solutions (CES) team is responsible for the management of non-financial risks associated with correspondent banking relationships. It assesses potential financial crime and reputational risks of these clients by conducting a holistic analysis of the risks they pose to Deutsche Bank. The team provides advice for business areas in relation to our clients' financial crime compliance programme and considers country-specific, reputational, and geopolitical / PEP risks of maintaining correspondent banking relationships with banks located across the world.Your key responsibilitiesLead thematic (sector or country-specific) or trigger CES-led correspondent banking reviews to gain an understanding of the client sector and jurisdiction risk by:Conducting preliminary analysis of the client and sector and recommending clients for further reviewConducting holistic analysis of banks; assessment of their Anti-Financial Crime (AFC) control and governance structureConducting AFC risk-based transaction analysis reviewsBeing the author and owner of the formal assessment reportProvide financial crime advisory advice based on results of client reviewsPresenting report and formal findings to the appropriate governance councils.Collaborate with Regional CES Team Leads, as well as the local, regional, and global business and AFC network with respect to your own responsibilities, and leading onsite visits with the business at our clients' offices or via conference callsProvision of timely updates and escalation of issues where required to Global Head of CESProvide regular reports to the senior management on the status of non-financial risks, control effectiveness, and compliance mattersYour skills and experiencesMinimum of 7 years of Financial Crime Compliance experience gained from working in a financial institution, with exposure to correspondent banking and good understanding of local and / or international regulatory requirements related to AFC and compliance.Strong knowledge of the AFC control and governance framework implemented within banks including understanding of typical AML and Know Your Client and Sanctions policy/programme requirements (e.g. experience with Transactional Monitoring and Sanctions screening systems).Strong knowledge of SWIFT network and the financial crime risks of processing correspondent bank paymentsExperience working within a global team in a multinational organisation with proven experience in senior stakeholder management engagementHigh level of initiative, strong work ethic and analytical skills, with excellent attention to detail, plus able to work independently to manage deliverables to timely completion.Due to client segment and nature of the role, proficiency in both spoken and written English is required.    - Hybrid: While the job posting mentions full-time and part-time options, it also suggests that some flexibility in working arrangements will be offered (e.g., "Flexible Arbeitszeitmodelle").
```

```
5. Growth potential assessment:
   - High: The company offers various training programs, mental health awareness trainings, and opportunities for professional growth through networking, shared assessment programs, and participation in additional key control projects.
```

**RESPONSE:**
```
Here's an analysis of the job posting:

**Top 5 Required Skills/Qualifications:**

1. **Financial Crime Compliance experience**: Minimum 7 years of experience in a financial institution, with exposure to correspondent banking and good understanding of local/international regulatory requirements.
2. **Knowledge of AFC control and governance framework**: Strong knowledge of Anti-Financial Crime (AFC) control and governance structure implemented within banks, including AML and Know Your Client and Sanctions policy/programme requirements.
3. **SWIFT network expertise**: Experience with SWIFT network and financial crime risks of processing correspondent bank payments.
4. **Analytical skills and attention to detail**: High level of initiative, strong work ethic, analytical skills, and excellent attention to detail.
5. **Senior stakeholder management experience**: Proven experience in senior stakeholder management engagement within a global team.

**Company Culture Indicators:**

1. Emphasis on diversity, equity, and inclusion.
2. Focus on mental health awareness and consultation services.
3. Offerings for physical well-being (health check-ups, vaccination drives, advice on healthy living and nutrition).
4. Flexible working arrangements (part-time, hybrid working, job tandem).
5. Recognition of employee achievements and celebrations.

**Role Complexity Level:**

Junior-Mid

The role requires significant experience in financial crime compliance, analytical skills, and stakeholder management. However, the structure of the job posting suggests that the candidate will be working within a team, leading thematic reviews, and providing expert advice, which indicates a mid-level complexity.

**Remote Work Compatibility:**

Hybrid (Yes/No)

The job posting mentions "flexible working" arrangements, including part-time and hybrid working. However, it does not explicitly state whether the role is fully remote or requires regular in-office presence.

**Growth Potential Assessment:**

High

Given the focus on leading thematic reviews, providing expert advice, and collaborating with senior stakeholders, this role appears to have significant growth potential within Deutsche Bank. The company's emphasis on employee development and recognition also suggests a commitment to supporting career advancement.
```

## üî¨ Methodology

### Evaluation Framework
- **Version:** Sandy LLM Evaluation v1.0
- **Test Data:** Real job posting descriptions from Sandy database
- **Prompt Template:** Standardized job analysis prompt
- **Metrics:** Response quality, consistency, and performance timing
- **Transparency:** Complete prompt/response logging for reproducibility

### Data Processing
1. Job postings loaded from Sandy JSON files
2. Standardized prompts generated for each job
3. All models tested with identical prompts
4. Responses collected with timing and token metrics
5. Performance analysis and ranking generated

### Reproducibility
- All prompts and responses logged
- Evaluation configuration documented
- Results timestamped and versioned
- Framework code available for review
